        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1283988251" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16618440178960483196">***<strong><a href='http://www.twirlingpages.com/2016/09/23/review-heartless-marissa-meyer/' rel='nofollow noopener'>FULL REVIEW</a> ORIGINALLY AT <a href='http://www.twirlingpages.com/' rel='nofollow noopener'>www.twirlingpages.com!</a></strong><br/><br/><b>marissa meyer twisted together a tale that is different, and yet familiar.</b><br/><br/>i had high expectations going on HEARTLESS. marissa meyer is one of my favorite authors and ALICE IN WONDERLAND is one of my favorite stories. naturally, the mix would be amazing. but this book is <em>nothing</em> like <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/series/62018' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>THE LUNAR CHRONICLES</a>, and <strong>this story is not your ordinary retelling.</strong> i came to love the story and its characters, but i do have some minor complaints. <br/><br/>before beginni</span>
  <span id="freeText16618440178960483196" style="display:none">***<strong><a href="http://www.twirlingpages.com/2016/09/23/review-heartless-marissa-meyer/" rel="nofollow noopener">FULL REVIEW</a> ORIGINALLY AT <a href="http://www.twirlingpages.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">www.twirlingpages.com!</a></strong><br /><br /><b>marissa meyer twisted together a tale that is different, and yet familiar.</b><br /><br />i had high expectations going on HEARTLESS. marissa meyer is one of my favorite authors and ALICE IN WONDERLAND is one of my favorite stories. naturally, the mix would be amazing. but this book is <em>nothing</em> like <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/series/62018" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">THE LUNAR CHRONICLES</a>, and <strong>this story is not your ordinary retelling.</strong> i came to love the story and its characters, but i do have some minor complaints. <br /><br />before beginning, i’d recommend going over a wikipedia of what the original ALICE IN WONDERLAND story consists of. i knew a small basis – alice follows a rabbit down a hole and ends up in wonderland – but i didn’t bother with the details. i always imagined wonderland as a sort of place with a plethora of mysteries yet to be discovered. and so, i didn’t remember or care for minor characters. lemme say this again: KNOW THE ORIGIN STORY. not only will it make the book more enjoyable, but you’ll also be less confused. <strong>for the majority of the book, i was confused.</strong> but i didn’t mind so much because that’s wonderland. marissa meyer wrote the novel in a style that made me feel as if i <em>should</em> already know the world, but i didn’t. there were also (of course) parallels between the original tale.<br /><br />the writing style was <em>really</em> unexpected – and i loved it. everything from the characters to the setting to plot made the whole atmosphere feel so magical and wistful. <strong>i felt like i was IN wonderland and i was watching all the events string together.</strong> it took some getting used to – i was expecting something similar to TLC – but by the end i was in love. (and also drooling. don't read this book when you're hungry because the DESCRIPTIONS OF FOOD OMG. the main character is a baker and i just *sighs* I WANT THE FOOD.)<br /><br /><strong>what bothered me slightly about this novel was the pacing.</strong> i had a hard time getting into it (see: confusion) and when i did, there’d be chunks of chapters that were so sloooooooooow. there wasn’t much going on, and i couldn’t see where the focus was, and then BAM last hundred pages had me clutching the book like it was a missing arm. suddenly, i realize i love all the characters and the plot clicks into place. BUT i do think the climax could’ve come earlier in the book because it went from snail’s-pace to sofastsofast. although when the climax was revealed, i was an emotional wreck. <strong>marissa meyer can be SO HEARTLESS sometimes.</strong> (pun intended)<br /><br />HEARTLESS was a bit of a weird read for me. there were so many aspects i loved about the book – the characters, writing, plot, etc. – but the pacing and world threw me off. however, i also feel it’s partially my fault because i had expectations of what the story might be or “should” be. <strong>like wonderland, this book is not one you can predict.</strong> there are twists and tricks and turns and flips; so sit back, relax, and enjoy the story – because i’m sure you’ll have sympathy for the so-called evil queen of hearts by the end of the journey.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16618440178960483196" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1643974750" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1643974750" />
    <a title="Drew" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22104588-drew"><img alt="Drew" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1498412758p2/22104588.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1643974750?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Drew" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Drew" href="/user/show/22104588-drew">Drew</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22104588-drew?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22104588-drew?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/22104588-drew?shelf=retellings">retellings</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1643974750" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1757187596576498083"><blockquote>
  <i>“If ever I get married, I want there to be romance, and passion. I want to fall in love.”</i>
</blockquote><br/>4 1/2 stars. <b>This book broke my heart.</b> What a cruel ending. And yet, I saw it coming the whole time, which probably made it even harder to bear.<br/><br/>Oh my goodness, this book! I loved it so much and I think I'm in danger of becoming a hardcore Marissa Meyer fan. Like, I want to go to her house and demand she write a sequel. And bring a certain character back to life. *sobs*<br/><br/><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18584855.Heartless' title='Heartless by Marissa Meyer' rel='nofollow noopener'>Heartless</a> is an <s>evil, torturous</s> addi</span>
  <span id="freeText1757187596576498083" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>“If ever I get married, I want there to be romance, and passion. I want to fall in love.”</i>
</blockquote><br />4 1/2 stars. <b>This book broke my heart.</b> What a cruel ending. And yet, I saw it coming the whole time, which probably made it even harder to bear.<br /><br />Oh my goodness, this book! I loved it so much and I think I'm in danger of becoming a hardcore Marissa Meyer fan. Like, I want to go to her house and demand she write a sequel. And bring a certain character back to life. *sobs*<br /><br /><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/18584855.Heartless" title="Heartless by Marissa Meyer" rel="nofollow noopener">Heartless</a> is an <s>evil, torturous</s> addictive, clever retelling of <i>Alice in Wonderland.</i> It follows the Queen of Hearts' backstory—how did she become a tyrannic ruler with the bad habit of beheading people?<br /><br />Meet Catherine, the daughter of a Marquess, who loves to bake and has every intention of opening up her own bakery. But her parents have other ideas and want her to marry the King of Hearts, who has taken an interest in her. Cath suddenly finds herself whisked into a courtship with the silly, unintelligent King, while at the same time falling for Jest, the King's Joker.<br /><br />I loved the romance so much. Jest was ridiculously sexy and had me swooning nearly the minute his character was introduced. There was so much chemistry between Cath and he; I wanted Cath to find a way to marry Jest and understood her frustration toward her parents, who only cared about Cath becoming Queen.<br /><br />There were many other wonderful characters such as Cheshire, Hatta, and Raven that held similarities to the original characters with <b>Meyer's own unique spin.</b> In an imaginative, dreamlike world full of quests, prophecies, kingdoms, forbidden love, and sweets that made my mouth water, the twisty plot took different directions and was <b>full of so much goodness.</b> Individual scenes were perfection and I loved the touches of humor that reminded me of The Lunar Chronicles.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Are you here for a reason, Cheshire?”<br />“Why, yes, I would enjoy a cup of tea. I take mine with lots of cream, and no tea.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Probably the best thing—though it was also the most heartbreaking—was Cath's gradual unraveling of a smart, headstrong, lovable girl into a <b>cold, ruthless Queen.</b> I knew it was coming, but I was never quite prepared for it. The ending was dark and gory and Cath's change was a disturbing one. I think it shows the sign of a good writer when you find yourself able to care so deeply about a villain.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“She spoke without feeling, unburdened by love or dreams or the pain of a broken heart. It was a new day in Hearts, and she was the Queen.”</i>
</blockquote><br /><b>A new, exciting take on Lewis Carroll's world.</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="1757187596576498083" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1454045029" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1454045029" />
    <a title="Dana Kenedy (Dana and the Books)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books"><img alt="Dana Kenedy (Dana and the Books)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1464902542p2/372001.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1454045029?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dana Kenedy (Dana and the Books)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dana Kenedy (Dana and the Books)" href="/user/show/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books">Dana Kenedy (Dana and the Books)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books?shelf=2016-release">2016-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books?shelf=read-in-2017">read-in-2017</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books?shelf=2017-release">2017-release</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/372001-dana-kenedy-dana-and-the-books?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1454045029" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11394329953731201507">This review can also be found <a href='http://danaandthebooks.com/2017/03/08/review-heartless-marissa-meyer/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>on my blog, Dana and the Books</a>.<br/><br/><br/>Marissa Meyer has recently become one of my honoured auto-buy authors.<a href='http://danaandthebooks.com/2015/07/30/cinder-by-marissa-meyer-yes-yes-yes/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'> I read <em>Cinder</em> about a year and half ago</a>, not really expecting much, and surprised myself by obsessing and devouring the rest of the Lunar Chronicles Books in record time.<br/><br/>I read <em>Alice in Wonderland</em> ten years ago and the Disney movie was one of my favourites when I was little. So, given that Heartless is an origin story for the Queen of Hearts written by Queen Marissa</span>
  <span id="freeText11394329953731201507" style="display:none">This review can also be found <a href="http://danaandthebooks.com/2017/03/08/review-heartless-marissa-meyer/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">on my blog, Dana and the Books</a>.<br /><br /><br />Marissa Meyer has recently become one of my honoured auto-buy authors.<a href="http://danaandthebooks.com/2015/07/30/cinder-by-marissa-meyer-yes-yes-yes/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"> I read <em>Cinder</em> about a year and half ago</a>, not really expecting much, and surprised myself by obsessing and devouring the rest of the Lunar Chronicles Books in record time.<br /><br />I read <em>Alice in Wonderland</em> ten years ago and the Disney movie was one of my favourites when I was little. So, given that Heartless is an origin story for the Queen of Hearts written by Queen Marissa Meyer, no surprises that this was pretty much <em>the</em> most anticipated read.<br /><br />Within just the first few chapters, I found myself constantly hungry due to the delicious food descriptions. Makes me wonder if Marissa Meyer is a great dessert chef herself!<br /> 
  <strong><br />"Why is a raven like a writing-desk?"</strong>
 <br /> <br /><br />Cath was a wonderful character, complex and torn with emotions, going from a kind and innocent girl to the harsh queen we know so well.<br /><br />The Cath/Jest romance could be categorized as instalove, but I do feel under the circumstances it worked. They meshed wonderfully and I was rooting for them from their very first meeting.<br /><br />All of this is set to the wonderful world of Hearts, a quirky world, and a delight to immerse myself in the weirdness!<br /><br />While I enjoyed <em>Heartless</em>, I didn't love it. It was not as magical as the Lunar Chronicles.  In <em>Cinder</em>, I was sucked in just by the first few chapters. With <em>Heartless</em>, I didn't have the desperate need to keep reading. I read it over the course of a few weeks (I read Cinder in pretty much one go).<br /> 
  <strong><br />"How different everything could have been if you had thought to ask me that before."</strong>
 <br /> <br /><br />However, the last fifty pages were heartbreaking and perfect.<br /><br />Marissa is a wonderfully witty author. Her style has become more pronounced in <em>Heartless</em> and I cannot wait for her upcoming book, <em>Renegades</em>.<br /><br />Thank you so much MyKindaBook for sending over a copy!  (<a href="https://www.bookdepository.com/Heartless-Mariss-Meyer/9781509814138/?a_aid=DanaAndTheBooks" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Book Depository</a> / <a href="http://amzn.to/2neacF9" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon US</a> / <a href="http://amzn.to/2miifkQ" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon Canada</a> / <a href="http://amzn.to/2ndRtJJ" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon UK</a>)<br /> 
  <strong><br />"Off with his head."</strong>
 <br /> </span>
  <a data-text-id="11394329953731201507" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('9FECGP2otMOhhuHeAk50XJAjTeXVhSz8Mdz3yCNewB8Hmud9PukXKJ5eyX9EUL6Zn3UhzwFEp6OagC4/ljL88Q==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('J3Egtt0Rg8q1AQHMxFZ7u/4QkpOFfDbR8KQrQMBjjMHUusXTHlAgIYrZKW2CSLF+8Ub+uVG9vY5b+PK3dQ+wLw==')})
  }
